    <div class="pluginPlaceholder" id="navbarPluginPlaceholder">
    </div>
   </div>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
    var _count = 0,
      MOBILE_MAX_WIDTH = 678,
      SOCIAL_MEDIA_MAX_WIDTH = 700,
      TABLET_MAX_WIDTH = 768;
    var navbarInterval = setInterval(function() {
        if(window.jQuery) {
            (function() {
                clearInterval(navbarInterval);

                var ww = $(window).width(),
                previousSize,
                previousDisplayOptions,
                // Makes the newly open submenu be on focus
                jumpTo = function(elem){
                    setTimeout(function(){
                        var new_position = $(elem).offset();
                        $("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: new_position.top - 36 }, 500);
                        return false;
                    }, 300);
                },
                
                isMobile = {
                    Android: function() {return navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i);},
                    BlackBerry: function() {return navigator.userAgent.match(/BlackBerry/i);},
                    iPhone: function() {return navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i);},
                    iPad: function() {return navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i);},
                    iOS: function() {return navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone|iPad|iPod/i);},
                    Opera: function() {return navigator.userAgent.match(/Opera Mini/i);},
                    Windows: function() {return navigator.userAgent.match(/IEMobile/i);},
                    any: function() {return (isMobile.Android() || isMobile.BlackBerry() || isMobile.iOS() || isMobile.Opera() || isMobile.Windows());}
                },
                openSubMenu = function(e) {
                    var href = $(this).attr('href'),
                        ref = $(this).attr('ref'),
                        isClosingMenu = $(this).parent("li").hasClass("hover"),
                        isTouchScreen = $('#navigationBar').hasClass('touch'),
                        elem;
                    
                    if (ww &lt;= MOBILE_MAX_WIDTH) { /* Mobile size */                        
                        if(!href || href == '' || href == '#') {
                            $(this).parent("li").toggleClass("hover");
                            if(isClosingMenu) {
                                elem = $($(this).parent().parent());
                            } else {
                                elem = $('#'+ref);
                            }
                            if(elem) {// Focus on the just open submenu
                                jumpTo(elem);
                            }                        
                        }
                        e.stopPropagation();
                    } else if (isTouchScreen) { /* Not mobile sized but touchscreen (iPad) */
                        // On touchscreen devices we need to simulate hover state with css
                        if(!href || href == '' || href == '#') {
                            
                            if($(this).parent('li').hasClass('hover')) {
                                // Item already has hover, so just toggle
                                $(this).parent("li").toggleClass("hover");
                            } else {
                                // Close all open dropdowns on the same level
                                $(this).parent().parent('ul').children('.hover').removeClass('hover');
                                $(this).parent("li").toggleClass("hover");  
                            }                           
                        }
                        e.stopPropagation();                        
                    }
                }, 
                isMobileSized = function(){
                  
                  if(ww &lt;= MOBILE_MAX_WIDTH || isMobile.iPhone()){
                    return true;
                  }else{
                    return false;
                  }
                },
                
                isTabletSized = function(){
                  
                  if(ww &lt;= TABLET_MAX_WIDTH || isMobile.iPad()){
                    return true;
                    
                  }else{
                    
                    return false;
                  }
                  
                },
                
                isSmallTabletSized = function(){
                  return (ww &lt;= SOCIAL_MEDIA_MAX_WIDTH); 
                }, 
                
                adjustMenu = function() {
                  
                    if (isMobileSized()) { /* Mobile size */
                        
                        $(".toggleMenu").css("display", "inline-block");
                        if (!$(".toggleMenu").hasClass("active")) {
                            $(".nav").hide();
                        } else {
                            $(".nav").css('display', 'block');
                        }
                        
                        var logoPxsFromRight = ($(window).width() / 2) - ($('.navbarlogo').width() / 2)
                        $('.navbarlogo').css('right', logoPxsFromRight+'px');    
                        if(!jQuery.jGestures) {
                            head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];                            
                            if(head){
                                script = document.createElement('script');
                                script.src =  "http://content.mqcdn.com/winston-641/cdn/jgestures/js/jgestures.min.js";
                                head.appendChild(script);
                            }
                        }
                        setSizeClassName('mobile-size');
                    
                    }else {
                    
                        $(".toggleMenu").css("display", "none");
                        $(".nav").css('display', 'inline-block');
                        $(".nav li").removeClass("hover");
                        
                        
                        if (isSmallTabletSized()) {
                          
                            setSizeClassName('tablet-size', { display: 'small'});
                        
                        }else if(isTabletSized()){
                          
                          setSizeClassName('tablet-size');
                          
                        }else {
                          
                            setSizeClassName('desktop-size');
                        }
                    }
                },
                
                fireEvent = function(value, options) {
                    var e = $.Event('navbar-boundary-changed', { size: value, options: options });
                    $('body').trigger(e);
                },
                
                setSizeClassName = function(className, options) {
                    if(className != previousSize || options != previousDisplayOptions) {
                        // Fire event just if boundary has been changed 
                        fireEvent(className, options);
                    }            
                    previousSize = className;
                    previousDisplayOptions = options;
                    $("#navigationBar").removeClass('desktop-size tablet-size mobile-size').addClass(className);
                    if(className == 'mobile-size') {
                        $('.navigationBarLinks').addClass('background_nav');
                        
                    } else { 
                        $('a.subMenuLink, a.sideMenuLink').unbind('click');
                        $('.navigationBarLinks').removeClass('background_nav');
                        $('.subMenu').attr('style', ''); // Remove styles set specific for mobile (if any)
                        $('.sideMenuMobile').css('display', 'none'); // Collapse all sideMenus opened (if any)
                        if($('.navbar-search-icon').hasClass('selected')) {
                            // Hide search bar if open 
                            $('.navbar-search-icon').toggleClass('selected');
                            $('#navigationBar .navbar-search').css('display', 'none');
                        }
                    }
                },
                
                toggleSearchBox = function() {
                    $('.navbar-search-icon').toggleClass('selected');
                    $('#navigationBar .navbar-search').slideToggle('fast');
                };                    
                
                
                $(".nav li a[id!='signin-link']").each(function() {
                    if ($(this).next().length &gt; 0) {
                        $(this).addClass("parent");
                    };
                })
                
                $(".toggleMenu").click(function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    $(this).toggleClass("active");
                    $(".nav").slideToggle('fast');
                });

                $('.navbar-search-icon').click(function(event) {
                    event.stopPropagation();
                    toggleSearchBox();
                });
                
                $(window).bind('resize orientationchange', function() {
                    ww = document.body.clientWidth;
                    adjustMenu();
                });
                
                // Identify if the browser has touch-screen support
                if (!("ontouchstart" in document.documentElement)) {
                    $('#navigationBar').addClass("no-touch");
                } else {
                    $('#navigationBar').addClass("touch");
                }
                
                var eventType = isMobile.any() === true ? 'tapone' : 'click';
                $('#navigationBar').on(eventType, '.navigationBarLinks li', function(e) {
                    if($('#navigationBar').hasClass('mobile-size')) {
                        var linkTag = $(this).children().filter('a')[0];
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        // simulating click that works in iPhone as well
                        var click_ev = document.createEvent("MouseEvent");
                        click_ev.initEvent("click", true, true);
                        linkTag.dispatchEvent(click_ev);
                    }
                });
                
                $('#navigationBar').on('click', '.nav li a', openSubMenu);
                
                $('#navigationBar').on('click', 'a.subMenuLink, a.sideMenuLink', function() {
                    if (ww &lt;= MOBILE_MAX_WIDTH) { /* Mobile size */
                        $($($(this).parent()).children().filter('ul')[0]).slideToggle('fast');
                    }
                });
                
                adjustMenu();
                // Hides address bar on iPhone
                window.scrollTo(0,1);
                // Avoid non-responsive navbar flashing before the mobile navbar kicks in
                var navbar = document.getElementById('navigationBar');
                navbar.style.display = 'block';
                
                // Script to lazy load Send2Cell widget
                var navigationBar = document.getElementById('navigationBar'),
                    links = navigationBar.getElementsByTagName('a'),
                    done = false,
                    i, isSend2Cell, send2CellTitle, send2CellMessage, script, head,
    
                loadS2CWidget = function(mobileLink, send2CellTitle, send2CellMessage){
                    window.mc.s2c.id(11).key("ao1kb7Gw0lAN_9_f")
                        .title(send2CellTitle)
                        .message(send2CellMessage)
                        .iconUrl("http://content.mqcdn.com/winston-641/cdn/dotcom3/images/MQ_Send2Cell_logo.png")
                        .linkUrl(mobileLink.getAttribute('href')) /* link */
                        .roundIcon("false")
                        .linkColor("#009ADE")
                        .textColor("434343")
                        .sendColorLight("#8CC63F")
                        .sendColorDark("#638e2a")
                        .show();                        
                },
    
                onClickEventFactory = function(mobileLink, send2CellTitle, send2CellMessage){
                    return function(event){
                        if(!window.jQuery){
                            return true;
                        }
                        // Dont open widget when in mobile version
                        if($('#navigationBar').hasClass('mobile-size')) {
                            return true;
                        }
                        
                        if(window.mc &amp;&amp; window.mc.s2c){
                            loadS2CWidget(mobileLink, send2CellTitle, send2CellMessage);
                        } else {
                            head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
    
                            if(head){
                                script = document.createElement('script');
                                script.src = "/cdn/loader.js.pre$locale=en_US&amp;profile=send2cell";
                                script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = function(){
                                    if(!done &amp;&amp; (!this.readyState || this.readyState === "loaded" || this.readyState === "complete")){
                                        done = true;
                                        window.setTimeout(function(){
                                            loadS2CWidget(mobileLink, send2CellTitle, send2CellMessage);
                                        }, 500);
    
                                        // Handle memory leak in IE
                                        script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = null;
                                        if (head &amp;&amp; script.parentNode) {
                                            head.removeChild(script);
                                        }
                                    }
                                };
    
                                head.appendChild(script);
                            }
                        }
                        event = event || window.event;
                        if(event.preventDefault) {
                            event.preventDefault();
                        } else {
                            event.returnValue = false;
                        }
                        return false;
                    };
                };

                /* FIXME: There is  no better way of selecting mobile
                          linke until we add ids to navbar elements
                */
    
                for(i = 0; i &lt; links.length; i++){
                    send2CellTitle = links[i].getAttribute('send2CellTitle');
                    send2CellMessage = links[i].getAttribute('send2CellMessage');
                    isSend2Cell = links[i].getAttribute('send2cell');
    
                    if(isSend2Cell &amp;&amp; isSend2Cell === 'true' &amp;&amp; send2CellTitle &amp;&amp; send2CellTitle !== 'null' &amp;&amp; send2CellMessage &amp;&amp; send2CellMessage !== 'null'){
                        links[i].onclick = onClickEventFactory(links[i], send2CellTitle, send2CellMessage);
                    }
                }                    
                
            })();            
        }
        
        _count += 1;
        if(_count &gt; 20) {
            var navbar = document.getElementById('navigationBar');
            navbar.className += ' desktop-size no-touch';
            navbar.style.display = 'block';
            clearInterval(navbarInterval);
        }
    }, 100);
})();
   </script>
  </div>

   /*&lt;![CDATA[*/
    #navigationBar { z-index: 666; }
    #navigationBar.mobile-size #navbar-product-separator,
    #navigationBar.mobile-size .separator-product { display: block; }
  /*]]&gt;*/
  </style>

   <style>

     <div class="content-block clearfix article" id="article-view">
      <p>
       <a href="http://dsc.mapquest.com/files/2012/11/route-66-sm.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="alignleft size-full wp-image-511" height="322" src="http://dsc.mapquest.com/files/2012/11/route-66-sm.jpg" title="route 66 sm" width="250"/>
       </a>
       Once Americas most famous road, Route 66 lives on as a gateway to the past, dotted with historic gas stations, neon signs, and quirky rest stops and motels. The iconic American road trip covers 2,451 miles from Chicago to Los Angeles. While many landmarks disappeared after the construction of the Interstate Highway system, here are a few that still stand today.
      </p>
      <h2>
       Illinois
      </h2>
      <p>
       Route 66 starts in
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/9295240#photo/87519" target="_blank" title="Grant Park, Chicago, IL">
        Grant Park
       </a>
       in downtown
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7523807#photo/5083" target="_blank" title="Chicago, IL">
        Chicago
       </a>
       , once home to the 1893 World Exposition. The 319-acre park houses a handful of Chicago cultural institutions worth seeing before hitting the road. Along with the Shedd Aquarium, the Art Institute of Chicago, and the Field Museum, the Buckingham Fountain remains a centerpiece of the park. The Beaux-Arts fountain, dedicated in 1927, puts on a jetted water display every 20 minutes, April through October.
      </p>
      <p>
       Snap a photo of the historic Begin Route 66 sign on E. Adams Street, just west of Michigan Avenue. Leave hungry because one of the first stops along the route is
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/14349927#photo/87531" target="_blank" title="Dell Rhea's Chicken Basket">
        Dell Rheas Chicken Basket
       </a>
       , about 20 miles southwest of downtown in
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7021868#photo/87537" target="_blank" title="Hinsdale, IL">
        Hinsdale
       </a>
       . With the tagline Get your chicks on Route 66, the restaurant grew out of a gas station lunch counter, eventually transforming its two car repair bays into a full dining room.
      </p>
      <p>
       Though a fill-up might not be in order just yet, stop at one of the cottage-like former gas stations along the way like Amblers Texaco in
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/11855791#photo/87572" target="_blank" title="Dwight, IL">
        Dwight
       </a>
       , Standard Oil in
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8067626#photo/87574" target="_blank" title="Odell, IL">
        Odell
       </a>
       , or
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8877504#photo/87585" target="_blank" title="Soulsby Station Mount Olive, IL">
        Soulsby Station in Mt. Olive
       </a>
       , each designed with a sloped roof, white siding, and a canopy for cars to aesthetically fit into a new suburban America.
      </p>
      <p>
       Find Great Hotel Deals in Chicago.
       <br/>
       <a href="http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Chicago%2C+IL&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715">
        <img alt="" class="alignnone" height="31" src="http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg" title="Book Now" width="97"/>
       </a>
      </p>
      <h2>
       Missouri
      </h2>
      <p>
       About 90 minutes from St. Louis, the Wagon Wheel Motel in
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8082243#photo/87613" target="_blank" title="Cuba, MO">
        Cuba, Missouri
       </a>
       offers weary travelers overnight stays in stone cottages just as it has since 1936. Though the motel still has its classic neon sign, the rooms have been upgraded with HDTVs and wi-fi internet. Single rooms start at $55 per night.
      </p>
      <p>
       Just east of the Kansas and Oklahoma borders, the 66 Drive-In in
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7530922#photo/87618" target="_blank" title="Carthage, MO">
        Carthage, Missouri
       </a>
       preserves a favorite American form of entertainment. Opened in 1949, the drive-in theatre still showcases its original, 66-foot high movie screen that shows first-run films Friday through Sunday, April through October. Tickets go on sale at 8 p.m., and cost $7 for adults and $3 for children 12 and under.
      </p>
      <p>
       Find Great Hotel Deals In St. Louis.
       <br/>
       <a href="http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Saint Louis%2C+MO&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715">
        <img alt="" class="alignnone" height="31" src="http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg" title="Book Now" width="97"/>
       </a>
      </p>
      <h2>
       Kansas
      </h2>
      <p>
       Though Route 66 may be better known for its diners and restaurants, the Willams Store in
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/11768236" target="_blank" title="Riverton, KS">
        Riverton
       </a>
       gave travelers an alternative by offering groceries, ice, clothing, and other staples. Today known as the
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/17538690#photo/87649" target="_blank" title="Old Riverton Store">
        Eisler Bros. Old Riverton Store
       </a>
       , the red brick building still serves travelers as a market and general store, stocked with Route 66 souvenirs.
      </p>
      <p>
       Five miles south, the Rainbow Bridge in
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8043234#photo/87650" target="_blank" title="Baxter Springs, KS">
        Baxter Springs
       </a>
       still stands as a working monument to the engineering innovations that made Route 66 possible. Though the main road traffic has been re-routed for preservation efforts, the arched 130-foot bridge is still accessibleand driveableon a one-way road.
      </p>
      <h2>
       Oklahoma
      </h2>
      <p>
       Route 66 may be best known for creating roadside attractions with oversized or memorable icons visible from the road. One of these, Oklahoma Citys Milk Bottle Grocery, will be instantly recognized thanks to the supersized milk bottle on the one-story buildings roof. Today the building itself houses
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/15074604#photo/87652" target="_blank" title="Saigon Baguette">
        Saigon Baguette
       </a>
       , a Vietnamese sandwich shop, but the milk bottle still stands above.
      </p>
      <p>
       Find Great Hotel Deals in Oklahoma City.
       <br/>
       <a href="http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Oklahoma City%2C+OK&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715">
        <img alt="" class="alignnone" height="31" src="http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg" title="Book Now" width="97"/>
       </a>
      </p>
      <h2>
       Texas
      </h2>
      <p>
       Route 66 only runs across the top of the Texas panhandle, but the route created bustling business in places like
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/12543905" target="_blank" title="McLean, TX">
        McLean
       </a>
       . Though mostly abandoned today, the McLean commercial district maintains its distinct mid-century style in the building storefronts and canopied gas stations. The Texas Route 66 Museum in McLean shows off old signs, photos, and other mementos Tuesday through Saturday 10 a.m. to 4 p.m.
      </p>
      <h2>
       New Mexico
      </h2>
      <p>
       In New Mexicos largest city of
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7529440#photo/87679" target="_blank" title="Albuquerque, NM">
        Albuquerque
       </a>
       , Route 66 has left a lasting mark. A handful of motels like the
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/9579808" target="_blank" title="Tewa Lodge">
        Tewa Lodge
       </a>
       remain open for overnight visitors, and the Nob Hill Shopping Center has endured as a lively retail area despite competition from indoor malls.
      </p>
      <p>
       About 45 miles west of Albuquerque, the
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/15771360#photo/87717" target="_blank" title="Pueblo of Laguna">
        Pueblo of Laguna
       </a>
       captures an even older period of American history. The Pueblo people have inhabited the land since 1300, and buildings dating from the 1400s still stand. The St. Joseph Church, built in 1701, is usually open to visitors Monday through Friday from 9 a.m. to 3 p.m.
      </p>
      <p>
       Find Great Hotel Deals In Albuquerque.
       <br/>
       <a href="http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Albuquerque%2C+NM&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715">
        <img alt="" class="alignnone" height="31" src="http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg" title="Book Now" width="97"/>
       </a>
      </p>
      <h2>
       Arizona
      </h2>
      <p>
       One of the more unique motels along Route 66, the
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/1308262#photo/5608" target="_blank" title="Wigwam Village Motel">
        Wigwam Village Motel in Holbrook
       </a>
       gives visitors the chance to sleep in a 28-foot high teepee. The 15 steel and concrete rooms have original furniture, as well as a full bathroom. Rooms cost $52 for one double bed and $58 for two beds.
      </p>
      <p>
       Much like many once-thriving towns along Route 66,
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7535142#photo/87791" target="_blank" title="Kingman, AZ">
        Kingman, Arizona
       </a>
       suffered an initial decline after the completion of Interstate 40, but this city has recently seen an increase in new residents and businesses. The Powerhouse Visitor Center, housed in the towns former electrical powerhouse, includes a Route 66 museum with life-sized dioramas and murals depicting the regions history.
      </p>
      <h2>
       California
      </h2>
      <p>
       A number of people took Route 66 not just as a road trip, but a chance to start a new life in the agriculturally booming California. The Harvey House Railroad Depot in
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/11822040" target="_blank" title="Barstow, CA">
        Barstow
       </a>
       chronicles the parallels between the railroad and the highway in its Route 66 Mother Road Museum, open 11 a.m. to 4 p.m. Friday through Sunday.
      </p>
      <p>
       Pass over the Colorado Street Bridge in Pasadena to see another engineering feat of its day. The 150-foot tall bridge crosses the Arroyo Seco stream using support columns between extensive arches, and maintains artistic touches like cast-iron lampposts and decorative concrete railings.
      </p>
      <p>
       At one point, Route 66 ended in downtown
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7534051" target="_blank" title="Los Angeles, CA">
        Los Angeles
       </a>
       at Broadway and 7th Street. It was then extended to the intersection of Lincoln and Olympic Boulevard in Santa Monica, but tourists and the Route 66 Alliance have claimed
       <a href="http://discover.mapquest.com/places/3872961" target="_blank" title="Santa Monica Pier, CA">
        Santa Monica Pier
       </a>
       as the honorary end, as the views of the Pacific offer a spectacular sight symbolic of a journey well-trodden.
      </p>
      <p>
       Find Great Hotel Deals in Los Angeles.
       <br/>
       <a href="http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Los Angeles%2C+CA&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715">
        <img alt="" class="alignnone" height="31" src="http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg" title="Book now" width="97"/>
       </a>
      </p>
     </div>

         <p class="comment-body">
          In Arizona you missed one of the greatest treat. The stop at the ghost town Oatman with its mules and the fantastic scenery continuing East.
         </p>

      MQ2.Utils.GoogleAnalytics.initialize("COLLECTION_PAGE");
    
      var collection = new MQ2.Models.Collection({"type":"collection","name":"Driving Discovery: Historic Route 66 Road Trip","owner_name":"MapQuest Feature Writer Lindsey Galloway","owner_avatar_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/1842ae6b2c6f826a5b7affe148b36b4d","id":715,"description":"The Historic Route 66 road trip covers a swath of America from Illinois to California. See the Route 66 landmarks that have stood the test of time.","path":"/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715","total_likes":425,"total_photos":95,"branding_details":{"ad_magic_number":"93329696","article_content":"&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://dsc.mapquest.com/files/2012/11/route-66-sm.jpg\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignleft size-full wp-image-511\" title=\"route 66 sm\" src=\"http://dsc.mapquest.com/files/2012/11/route-66-sm.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"250\" height=\"322\" /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;Once America\u2019s most famous road, Route 66 lives on as a gateway to the past, dotted with historic gas stations, neon signs, and quirky rest stops and motels. The iconic American road trip covers 2,451 miles from Chicago to Los Angeles. While many landmarks disappeared after the construction of the Interstate Highway system, here are a few that still stand today.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Illinois&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Route 66 starts in &lt;a title=\"Grant Park, Chicago, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/9295240#photo/87519\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Grant Park&lt;\/a&gt; in downtown &lt;a title=\"Chicago, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7523807#photo/5083\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Chicago&lt;\/a&gt;, once home to the 1893 World Exposition. The 319-acre park houses a handful of Chicago cultural institutions worth seeing before hitting the road. Along with the Shedd Aquarium, the Art Institute of Chicago, and the Field Museum, the Buckingham Fountain remains a centerpiece of the park. The Beaux-Arts fountain, dedicated in 1927, puts on a jetted water display every 20 minutes, April through October.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Snap a photo of the historic \u201cBegin Route 66\u201d sign on E. Adams Street, just west of Michigan Avenue. Leave hungry because one of the first stops along the route is &lt;a title=\"Dell Rhea's Chicken Basket\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/14349927#photo/87531\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Dell Rhea\u2019s Chicken Basket&lt;\/a&gt;, about 20 miles southwest of downtown in &lt;a title=\"Hinsdale, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7021868#photo/87537\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Hinsdale&lt;\/a&gt;. With the tagline \u201cGet your chicks on Route 66,\u201d the restaurant grew out of a gas station lunch counter, eventually transforming its two car repair bays into a full dining room.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Though a fill-up might not be in order just yet, stop at one of the cottage-like former gas stations along the way like Ambler\u2019s Texaco in &lt;a title=\"Dwight, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/11855791#photo/87572\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Dwight&lt;\/a&gt;, Standard Oil in &lt;a title=\"Odell, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8067626#photo/87574\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Odell&lt;\/a&gt;, or &lt;a title=\"Soulsby Station Mount Olive, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8877504#photo/87585\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Soulsby Station in Mt. Olive&lt;\/a&gt;, each designed with a sloped roof, white siding, and a canopy for cars to aesthetically fit into a new suburban America.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Hotel Deals in Chicago.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Chicago%2C+IL&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignnone\" title=\"Book Now\" src=\"http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"97\" height=\"31\" /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Missouri&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;About 90 minutes from St. Louis, the Wagon Wheel Motel in &lt;a title=\"Cuba, MO\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8082243#photo/87613\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Cuba, Missouri&lt;\/a&gt; offers weary travelers overnight stays in stone cottages just as it has since 1936. Though the motel still has its classic neon sign, the rooms have been upgraded with HDTVs and wi-fi internet. Single rooms start at $55 per night.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Just east of the Kansas and Oklahoma borders, the 66 Drive-In in &lt;a title=\"Carthage, MO\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7530922#photo/87618\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Carthage, Missouri &lt;\/a&gt;preserves a favorite American form of entertainment. Opened in 1949, the drive-in theatre still showcases its original, 66-foot high movie screen that shows first-run films Friday through Sunday, April through October. Tickets go on sale at 8 p.m., and cost $7 for adults and $3 for children 12 and under.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Hotel Deals In St. Louis.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Saint Louis%2C+MO&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignnone\" title=\"Book Now\" src=\"http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"97\" height=\"31\" /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Kansas&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Though Route 66 may be better known for its diners and restaurants, the Willams\u2019 Store in &lt;a title=\"Riverton, KS\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/11768236\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Riverton&lt;\/a&gt; gave travelers an alternative by offering groceries, ice, clothing, and other staples. Today known as the &lt;a title=\"Old Riverton Store\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/17538690#photo/87649\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Eisler Bros. Old Riverton Store&lt;\/a&gt;, the red brick building still serves travelers as a market and general store, stocked with Route 66 souvenirs.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Five miles south, the Rainbow Bridge in &lt;a title=\"Baxter Springs, KS\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8043234#photo/87650\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Baxter Springs&lt;\/a&gt; still stands as a working monument to the engineering innovations that made Route 66 possible. Though the main road traffic has been re-routed for preservation efforts, the arched 130-foot bridge is still accessible\u2014and driveable\u2014on a one-way road.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Oklahoma&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Route 66 may be best known for creating roadside attractions with oversized or memorable icons visible from the road. One of these, Oklahoma City\u2019s Milk Bottle Grocery, will be instantly recognized thanks to the supersized milk bottle on the one-story building\u2019s roof. Today the building itself houses &lt;a title=\"Saigon Baguette\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/15074604#photo/87652\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Saigon Baguette&lt;\/a&gt;, a Vietnamese sandwich shop, but the milk bottle still stands above.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Hotel Deals in Oklahoma City.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Oklahoma City%2C+OK&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignnone\" title=\"Book Now\" src=\"http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"97\" height=\"31\" /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Texas&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Route 66 only runs across the top of the Texas panhandle, but the route created bustling business in places like &lt;a title=\"McLean, TX\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/12543905\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;McLean&lt;\/a&gt;. Though mostly abandoned today, the McLean commercial district maintains its distinct mid-century style in the building storefronts and canopied gas stations. The Texas Route 66 Museum in McLean shows off old signs, photos, and other mementos Tuesday through Saturday 10 a.m. to 4 p.m.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;New Mexico&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;In New Mexico\u2019s largest city of &lt;a title=\"Albuquerque, NM\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7529440#photo/87679\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Albuquerque&lt;\/a&gt;, Route 66 has left a lasting mark. A handful of motels like the&lt;a title=\"Tewa Lodge\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/9579808\" target=\"_blank\"&gt; Tewa Lodge&lt;\/a&gt; remain open for overnight visitors, and the Nob Hill Shopping Center has endured as a lively retail area despite competition from indoor malls.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;About 45 miles west of Albuquerque, the &lt;a title=\"Pueblo of Laguna\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/15771360#photo/87717\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Pueblo of Laguna&lt;\/a&gt; captures an even older period of American history. The Pueblo people have inhabited the land since 1300, and buildings dating from the 1400s still stand. The St. Joseph Church, built in 1701, is usually open to visitors Monday through Friday from 9 a.m. to 3 p.m.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Hotel Deals In Albuquerque.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Albuquerque%2C+NM&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignnone\" title=\"Book Now\" src=\"http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"97\" height=\"31\" /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Arizona&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;One of the more unique motels along Route 66, the &lt;a title=\"Wigwam Village Motel\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/1308262#photo/5608\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Wigwam Village Motel in Holbrook&lt;\/a&gt; gives visitors the chance to sleep in a 28-foot high teepee. The 15 steel and concrete rooms have original furniture, as well as a full bathroom. Rooms cost $52 for one double bed and $58 for two beds.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Much like many once-thriving towns along Route 66, &lt;a title=\"Kingman, AZ\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7535142#photo/87791\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Kingman, Arizona&lt;\/a&gt; suffered an initial decline after the completion of Interstate 40, but this city has recently seen an increase in new residents and businesses. The Powerhouse Visitor Center, housed in the town\u2019s former electrical powerhouse, includes a Route 66 museum with life-sized dioramas and murals depicting the region\u2019s history.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;California&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;A number of people took Route 66 not just as a road trip, but a chance to start a new life in the agriculturally booming California. The Harvey House Railroad Depot in &lt;a title=\"Barstow, CA\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/11822040\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Barstow&lt;\/a&gt; chronicles the parallels between the railroad and the highway in its Route 66 Mother Road Museum, open 11 a.m. to 4 p.m. Friday through Sunday.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Pass over the Colorado Street Bridge in Pasadena to see another engineering feat of its day. The 150-foot tall bridge crosses the Arroyo Seco stream using support columns between extensive arches, and maintains artistic touches like cast-iron lampposts and decorative concrete railings.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;At one point, Route 66 ended in downtown &lt;a title=\"Los Angeles, CA\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7534051\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Los Angeles&lt;\/a&gt; at Broadway and 7th Street. It was then extended to the intersection of Lincoln and Olympic Boulevard in Santa Monica, but tourists and the Route 66 Alliance have claimed &lt;a title=\"Santa Monica Pier, CA\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/3872961\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Santa Monica Pier&lt;\/a&gt; as the honorary end, as the views of the Pacific offer a spectacular sight symbolic of a journey well-trodden.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Hotel Deals in Los Angeles.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Los Angeles%2C+CA&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715\"&gt;&lt;img /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;","article_id":"251","header_box_background_color":"#fcfdfd","header_box_text_color":"","hero_image_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/9dd146dc0faeacba3c0189dd4b42163d","id":122,"on_homepage":null,"page_background_color":"#06070f","show_in_ca":false,"show_in_us":true,"subheader_text_color":"","superhero_image_url":null,"tracking_pixel_1":null,"tracking_pixel_2":null,"video_id":null},"editorial":true,"travel_guide":true,"main_photo_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/8a979cb4ec7f6f5ca08b4ba367752528","collage_image_urls":["http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/614636469d4f860b41e1f81a6dd24401","http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/a548f949df724aa1dd0d8c9396271acb","http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/760d4f57a2cd0ef99b303cdd77355491"],"comment_service":{},"cover_photo_id":null,"owner":{"id":137,"avatar_url_small":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/1842ae6b2c6f826a5b7affe148b36b4d","avatar_url_large":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/1842ae6b2c6f826a5b7affe148b36b4d","passport_path":"/users/137","become_path":"/users/137/become","display_name":"MapQuest Feature Writer Lindsey Galloway","is_brand":true,"is_followed":false,"visit_count":0},"is_branded":true,"has_branding_details":true,"page_background_color":"#06070f","header_box_background_color":"#fcfdfd","header_box_text_color":"","subheader_text_color":"","hero_image_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/9dd146dc0faeacba3c0189dd4b42163d","article_id":"251","article_content":"&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://dsc.mapquest.com/files/2012/11/route-66-sm.jpg\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignleft size-full wp-image-511\" title=\"route 66 sm\" src=\"http://dsc.mapquest.com/files/2012/11/route-66-sm.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"250\" height=\"322\" /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;Once America\u2019s most famous road, Route 66 lives on as a gateway to the past, dotted with historic gas stations, neon signs, and quirky rest stops and motels. The iconic American road trip covers 2,451 miles from Chicago to Los Angeles. While many landmarks disappeared after the construction of the Interstate Highway system, here are a few that still stand today.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Illinois&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Route 66 starts in &lt;a title=\"Grant Park, Chicago, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/9295240#photo/87519\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Grant Park&lt;\/a&gt; in downtown &lt;a title=\"Chicago, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7523807#photo/5083\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Chicago&lt;\/a&gt;, once home to the 1893 World Exposition. The 319-acre park houses a handful of Chicago cultural institutions worth seeing before hitting the road. Along with the Shedd Aquarium, the Art Institute of Chicago, and the Field Museum, the Buckingham Fountain remains a centerpiece of the park. The Beaux-Arts fountain, dedicated in 1927, puts on a jetted water display every 20 minutes, April through October.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Snap a photo of the historic \u201cBegin Route 66\u201d sign on E. Adams Street, just west of Michigan Avenue. Leave hungry because one of the first stops along the route is &lt;a title=\"Dell Rhea's Chicken Basket\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/14349927#photo/87531\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Dell Rhea\u2019s Chicken Basket&lt;\/a&gt;, about 20 miles southwest of downtown in &lt;a title=\"Hinsdale, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7021868#photo/87537\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Hinsdale&lt;\/a&gt;. With the tagline \u201cGet your chicks on Route 66,\u201d the restaurant grew out of a gas station lunch counter, eventually transforming its two car repair bays into a full dining room.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Though a fill-up might not be in order just yet, stop at one of the cottage-like former gas stations along the way like Ambler\u2019s Texaco in &lt;a title=\"Dwight, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/11855791#photo/87572\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Dwight&lt;\/a&gt;, Standard Oil in &lt;a title=\"Odell, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8067626#photo/87574\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Odell&lt;\/a&gt;, or &lt;a title=\"Soulsby Station Mount Olive, IL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8877504#photo/87585\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Soulsby Station in Mt. Olive&lt;\/a&gt;, each designed with a sloped roof, white siding, and a canopy for cars to aesthetically fit into a new suburban America.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Hotel Deals in Chicago.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Chicago%2C+IL&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignnone\" title=\"Book Now\" src=\"http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"97\" height=\"31\" /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Missouri&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;About 90 minutes from St. Louis, the Wagon Wheel Motel in &lt;a title=\"Cuba, MO\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8082243#photo/87613\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Cuba, Missouri&lt;\/a&gt; offers weary travelers overnight stays in stone cottages just as it has since 1936. Though the motel still has its classic neon sign, the rooms have been upgraded with HDTVs and wi-fi internet. Single rooms start at $55 per night.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Just east of the Kansas and Oklahoma borders, the 66 Drive-In in &lt;a title=\"Carthage, MO\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7530922#photo/87618\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Carthage, Missouri &lt;\/a&gt;preserves a favorite American form of entertainment. Opened in 1949, the drive-in theatre still showcases its original, 66-foot high movie screen that shows first-run films Friday through Sunday, April through October. Tickets go on sale at 8 p.m., and cost $7 for adults and $3 for children 12 and under.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Hotel Deals In St. Louis.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Saint Louis%2C+MO&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignnone\" title=\"Book Now\" src=\"http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"97\" height=\"31\" /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Kansas&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Though Route 66 may be better known for its diners and restaurants, the Willams\u2019 Store in &lt;a title=\"Riverton, KS\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/11768236\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Riverton&lt;\/a&gt; gave travelers an alternative by offering groceries, ice, clothing, and other staples. Today known as the &lt;a title=\"Old Riverton Store\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/17538690#photo/87649\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Eisler Bros. Old Riverton Store&lt;\/a&gt;, the red brick building still serves travelers as a market and general store, stocked with Route 66 souvenirs.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Five miles south, the Rainbow Bridge in &lt;a title=\"Baxter Springs, KS\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8043234#photo/87650\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Baxter Springs&lt;\/a&gt; still stands as a working monument to the engineering innovations that made Route 66 possible. Though the main road traffic has been re-routed for preservation efforts, the arched 130-foot bridge is still accessible\u2014and driveable\u2014on a one-way road.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Oklahoma&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Route 66 may be best known for creating roadside attractions with oversized or memorable icons visible from the road. One of these, Oklahoma City\u2019s Milk Bottle Grocery, will be instantly recognized thanks to the supersized milk bottle on the one-story building\u2019s roof. Today the building itself houses &lt;a title=\"Saigon Baguette\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/15074604#photo/87652\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Saigon Baguette&lt;\/a&gt;, a Vietnamese sandwich shop, but the milk bottle still stands above.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Hotel Deals in Oklahoma City.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Oklahoma City%2C+OK&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignnone\" title=\"Book Now\" src=\"http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"97\" height=\"31\" /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Texas&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Route 66 only runs across the top of the Texas panhandle, but the route created bustling business in places like &lt;a title=\"McLean, TX\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/12543905\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;McLean&lt;\/a&gt;. Though mostly abandoned today, the McLean commercial district maintains its distinct mid-century style in the building storefronts and canopied gas stations. The Texas Route 66 Museum in McLean shows off old signs, photos, and other mementos Tuesday through Saturday 10 a.m. to 4 p.m.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;New Mexico&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;In New Mexico\u2019s largest city of &lt;a title=\"Albuquerque, NM\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7529440#photo/87679\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Albuquerque&lt;\/a&gt;, Route 66 has left a lasting mark. A handful of motels like the&lt;a title=\"Tewa Lodge\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/9579808\" target=\"_blank\"&gt; Tewa Lodge&lt;\/a&gt; remain open for overnight visitors, and the Nob Hill Shopping Center has endured as a lively retail area despite competition from indoor malls.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;About 45 miles west of Albuquerque, the &lt;a title=\"Pueblo of Laguna\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/15771360#photo/87717\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Pueblo of Laguna&lt;\/a&gt; captures an even older period of American history. The Pueblo people have inhabited the land since 1300, and buildings dating from the 1400s still stand. The St. Joseph Church, built in 1701, is usually open to visitors Monday through Friday from 9 a.m. to 3 p.m.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Hotel Deals In Albuquerque.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Albuquerque%2C+NM&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignnone\" title=\"Book Now\" src=\"http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"97\" height=\"31\" /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Arizona&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;One of the more unique motels along Route 66, the &lt;a title=\"Wigwam Village Motel\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/1308262#photo/5608\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Wigwam Village Motel in Holbrook&lt;\/a&gt; gives visitors the chance to sleep in a 28-foot high teepee. The 15 steel and concrete rooms have original furniture, as well as a full bathroom. Rooms cost $52 for one double bed and $58 for two beds.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Much like many once-thriving towns along Route 66, &lt;a title=\"Kingman, AZ\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7535142#photo/87791\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Kingman, Arizona&lt;\/a&gt; suffered an initial decline after the completion of Interstate 40, but this city has recently seen an increase in new residents and businesses. The Powerhouse Visitor Center, housed in the town\u2019s former electrical powerhouse, includes a Route 66 museum with life-sized dioramas and murals depicting the region\u2019s history.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;California&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;A number of people took Route 66 not just as a road trip, but a chance to start a new life in the agriculturally booming California. The Harvey House Railroad Depot in &lt;a title=\"Barstow, CA\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/11822040\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Barstow&lt;\/a&gt; chronicles the parallels between the railroad and the highway in its Route 66 Mother Road Museum, open 11 a.m. to 4 p.m. Friday through Sunday.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Pass over the Colorado Street Bridge in Pasadena to see another engineering feat of its day. The 150-foot tall bridge crosses the Arroyo Seco stream using support columns between extensive arches, and maintains artistic touches like cast-iron lampposts and decorative concrete railings.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;At one point, Route 66 ended in downtown &lt;a title=\"Los Angeles, CA\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7534051\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Los Angeles&lt;\/a&gt; at Broadway and 7th Street. It was then extended to the intersection of Lincoln and Olympic Boulevard in Santa Monica, but tourists and the Route 66 Alliance have claimed &lt;a title=\"Santa Monica Pier, CA\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/3872961\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Santa Monica Pier&lt;\/a&gt; as the honorary end, as the views of the Pacific offer a spectacular sight symbolic of a journey well-trodden.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Hotel Deals in Los Angeles.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Los Angeles%2C+CA&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/driving-discovery-historic-route-66-road-trip-715\"&gt;&lt;img Take the 10 to 15 minute ferry tour operated by Alcatraz Cruises from San Francisco\u2019s Pier 33 to discover the island\u2019s history, first as a Civil War citadel, and how the island has evolved since the prison\u2019s closure in 1963.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Alcatraz ferry rides run Monday through Sunday and leave about every half hour from 9 a.m. to 4 p.m. Tickets cost $28, but book early, especially in summer months where tickets sell out days in advance.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Plan at least two to three hours for a trip to Alcatraz. The ferry ticket includes a 45-minute audio walking tour of the cellhouse, narrated by former inmates and guards. After walking the grounds, take the time to walk the rest of the island to see the nesting seabirds like gulls, herons, and egrets (the name \u201cAlcatraz\u201d originates from the Spanish alcatraces or \u201cstrange birds\u201d that early settlers saw). Go from February through August for the best chance of seeing nesting and baby birds.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Park rangers also offer free programs throughout the day on the military, and natural history of the island, as well as talks on the 18-month American Indian occupation that occurred after the prison\u2019s closure, which resulted in significant federal policy changes toward American Indian autonomy in the U.S.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;For a more in-depth visit, take one of the $35 Alcatraz night tours departing Thursday through Monday at 6:10 p.m. or 6:45 p.m. The evening tour offers a more in-depth narration on the ferry ride over, as well as personally guided tours of the prison facility and cell door demonstrations. Some of the island remains closed at night for safety reasons, so those who want to wander on their own are better off taking an earlier tour. At the Iowa baseball field where they filmed scenes from the movie, visitors can bring bats and start a game, watch from the bleachers, or just disappear into the corn fields.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Hockey Hall of Fame in Toronto, Canada&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;See the Stanley Cup in its silver glory in the center hall (at least when it\u2019s not making the rounds with the NHL champions), or try defending against shots from Gretzky in a goalie simulator. Those up for a road trip can drive south to see the Unite Sates Hockey Hall of Fame in Eveleth, Minnesota to see the world\u2019s largest hockey stick, measuring 110 feet long and weighing over 10,000 pounds.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Olympic Training Center in Colorado Springs, Colorado&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;More than just a shrine to past glories, the Olympic Training Center hosts training athletes all year round in sports from gymnastics to skeet shooting. The 45-minute daily free tours of the center are also sometimes given by the athletes themselves who live on-site.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Lambeau Field, Green Bay, Wisconsin&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Sure, the pro-football Hall of Fame in Canton, Ohio has plenty to make an NFL fanatic faint, but for such a physical sport, there\u2019s not much to match the feeling of being on the field. So even non-Packer fans will love letting loose on Lambeau Field, the longest continually operating field in the NFL.\u00a0 Tours of the \u201cFrozen Tundra\u201d happen daily, except during home games, and cost $11.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;NASCAR Hall of Fame in Charlotte, North Carolina&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;This new addition to sports history opened in 2010 with more than 150,000 square feet dedicated to racing history (like the fact that NASCAR started as a way for bootleggers to outrun the cops during prohibition). ","path":"/collections/everydayer-the-augusta-golf-club-ga-723","total_likes":6,"total_photos":0,"branding_details":{"ad_magic_number":"93329696","article_content":"&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://dsc.mapquest.com/files/2012/11/golf-image.jpg\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignleft size-full wp-image-537\" title=\"golf image\" src=\"http://dsc.mapquest.com/files/2012/11/golf-image.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"386\" height=\"217\" /&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;With only about 300 members at any given time, the &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/4630044\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;August Golf Club&lt;\/a&gt; remains off-limits to the general public most of the year. But during the annual Masters Tournament, one of the four major professional golf tournaments, visitors have the chance to live vicariously through Tiger Woods, Phil Mickelson, and other top golf stars.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Augusta makes a limited number of tickets available to the public for the practice rounds and the tournament itself (held in early April). An online application for the tickets must be submitted by the end of July for the practice rounds, and by the end of June for tournament tickets for the following year\u2019s tournament. If selected in the random draw, practice round tickets cost $50 and daily tournament tickets cost $75.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Built in 1933, the golf course was once a plant nursery. Today, each of the 18 courses are named after different plant species from Juniper (Hole 6) to Camellia (Hole 10). The course has changed dramatically over the years, as different architects have added additional bunkers, water hazards, and trees. The Daily Tournament tickets give visitors a ground pass to see the courses and the golf game up close.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Don\u2019t miss the last day of the tournament when the club\u2019s famous green jacket is awarded to the winner of the tournament, who then becomes an honorary member of the club. Even in the absence of Masters tickets, visitors can get their golf fix any time of year at public golf courses like the Augusta Municipal Golf Course, Forest Hills Golf Club, and First Tee of Augusta. In addition to its golf pedigree, the city of Augusta (145 miles east of Atlanta on the South Carolina border) also has a rich artist community that appeals to golfers and non-golfers alike.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Artists\u2019 Row, running along Broad Street, houses a handful of galleries specializing in glass art, pottery, and painting. The Morris Museum, open Tuesday through Saturday 10 a.m. to 5 pm., and Sunday 12 p.m. to 5 p.m., showcases 200 years of art by Southern artists. During the 2012 Masters Tournament in Augusta, the museum dedicated an entire exhibition to images of golf in art, celebrating the intersection of the city\u2019s two great passions. ","path":"/collections/around-the-block-the-world-of-coca-cola-atlanta-559","total_likes":6,"total_photos":0,"branding_details":{"ad_magic_number":"93329696","article_content":"&lt;p&gt;Invented in 1886 by an Atlanta pharmacist, Coca-Cola has influenced the global beverage industry ever since. The soda\u2019s long and storied history plays out every day at &lt;a title=\"The World of Coca Cola Atlanta Georgia\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/14159307#photo/9882\"&gt;Atlanta, Georgia\u2019s World of Coca-Cola&lt;\/a&gt;, located in a palatial, 92,000 square-foot space just north of downtown.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The two-level monolith shows off the vault where the top secret Coca-Cola formula is stored, hundreds of red and white Coca-Cola signs and marketing materials, and a pop culture gallery documenting the brand\u2019s impact on American culture.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The \u201cTaste It\u201d exhibit, which features 60 different sodas from around the world, allows visitors to try different Coca-Cola-owned sodas famous in countries like France and Zimbabwe across six tasting stations. Touch-screen machines with more than 100 flavors can also be used to create new flavor combinations. Guests also get to take home a bottle of the classic Coca-Cola produced on-site in a traditional glass bottle.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The World of Coca-Cola in Atlanta is open Sunday through Thursday 10 a.m. to 6:30 p.m., and Friday and Saturday from 9 a.m. to 6:30 p.m. Tickets cost $16 for adults, $14 for seniors over 64, and $12 for children 12 and under. The self-guided tour takes about two hours, and VIP guided tours are offered three times a day at $26 a person. ","path":"/collections/the-long-haul-sun-soaked-adventures-on-kauai-6325","total_likes":8,"total_photos":58,"branding_details":{"ad_magic_number":"93329696","article_content":"&lt;p&gt;Hawai\u2019i means sun, sand, and chillin\u2019. It also means spring break for families and palm tree partiers alike. The tropical island archipelago has no shortage of sun-soaked options, but sorting out which island to spend it on can be a pain in paradise. But if the goal is surf, hike, and adventure, then bask in the beauty of &lt;a title=\"Kauai, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/5647503#photo/58332\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Kauai&lt;\/a&gt;, arguably Hawaii\u2019s most spectacular island.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The oldest and northernmost of the Hawaiian islands is also one of the most photogenic: Scenes from &lt;em&gt;Jurassic Park&lt;\/em&gt;, &lt;em&gt;Indiana Jones &lt;\/em&gt;and &lt;em&gt;The Descendants&lt;\/em&gt; were all filmed on Kauai. With its varied terrain, rolling waves and waterfalls, and kalaidescopic sunsets, Kauai is a living movie set for an adventure set in paradise. Follow this script to set up the perfect spring break scenes.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Coastal Cliffs of N\u0101 Pali &lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Hikers can\u2019t miss the 11-mile Kalalau Trail that runs through the &lt;a title=\"NaPali Coast, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/93147#photo/89437\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Na Pali Coast State Park&lt;\/a&gt;. Consistently rated the best coastal hike in the world, the trail starts at &lt;a title=\"Ke'e Beach, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/100901#photo/101799\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Ke\u2019e Beach&lt;\/a&gt;, on the north shore of the island, and ends a &lt;a title=\"Kalalau Beach, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/12426900\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Kalalau Beach&lt;\/a&gt;. With its five valleys, narrow paths, and muddy topsoil, the trail should be tackled by experienced hikers or with the help of a guide\u2014and don\u2019t forget your hiking boots, as the trail is not flip-flop friendly. Even well-heeled hikers often split the trek into two days, camping for a night in the &lt;a title=\"Hanakoa Valley, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/9543207\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Hanakoa Valley&lt;\/a&gt;, located at the 6-mile mark (snag the required $20 a person camping permit from the Hawaii State Parks Division in &lt;a title=\"Lihui, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/p/282039224\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Lihue&lt;\/a&gt; before heading out).&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The sometimes-treacherous journey pays dividends in the views of the towering cliffs, crashing surf, waterfalls, and the mile-long Kalalau Beach, all inaccessible by motor vehicles. Continue living unplugged even after the trail and book a condo at the &lt;a title=\"Hanalei Colony Resort, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/12790930\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Hanalei Colony Resort&lt;\/a&gt;, where rooms are TV, radio, and phone-free.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;The Grand Canyon of The Pacific&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;For an easier, but no less impressive, walking adventure, head toward the southwest side of the island to the &lt;a title=\"Waimea Canyon, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/93145#photo/117499\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Waimea Canyon&lt;\/a&gt;. Much like Arizona\u2019s version, \u201cThe Grand Canyon of the Pacific\u201d was carved by river currents and measures 10 miles long, a mile wide, and 3,600 feet deep. The red cliffs look much like their desert cousin, but with lush green dotting the eroded landscape.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The 0.3 mile Iliau Nature loop offers views of the canyons along with information about the native vegetation that grows along the basalt rock. The more difficult, 2.5-mile Kukui trail leads down the west side of the canyon, with a 2,000-ft elevation drop to the canyon floor.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Paddle Down The Wailua River&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Though Hawai\u2019i may be surrounded by water, Kauai is the only one of the islands to have navigable rivers. Water sports lovers can book a kayak or outrigger canoe and head down the 20-mile long &lt;a title=\"Wailua River State Park, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/93508\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Wailua River&lt;\/a&gt;, with a stop at the Fern Grotto. The natural lava-rock grotto earns its name thanks to the hanging ferns and foliage that make the secluded spot a lush escape.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;To see the river in one of its most beautiful states, make a trip to &lt;a title=\"Opaekaa Falls, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8292394\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Opaekaa Falls&lt;\/a&gt;. On the east side of the island, the falls are located only two miles up from Kuamoo Road and a roadside lookout makes for a panoramic photo spot.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Wildlife Watch at Poipu Beach Park &lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;As a complement to the crashing waves on Kauai\u2019s north shore, the south shore beaches can be as calm as a swimming pool, making these beaches ideal for families with younger children. Wind down with a stop at &lt;a title=\"Poipu Beach Park, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/93445#photo/1251\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Poipu Beach Park&lt;\/a&gt;, the island\u2019s most popular sandy beach for swimming, snorkeling, and bodyboarding. The calm waters also attract wildlife, especially December through May, when humpback whales, Hawaiian green sea turtles and endangered monk seals can be spotted swimming in the calm waters.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Some of Hawaii\u2019s best restaurants call the South Shore home as well. Order freshly caught ahi, ono, and mahi mahi from Merriman\u2019s Poipu or Roy\u2019s Poipu Bar and Grill, both restaurants started by founders of the Hawaii Regional Cuisine, the local farm-to-table movement started by 12 chefs in 1991.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Catch a parting shot of paradise while enjoying a classic mai tai or coconut mojito on the deck of the Beach House Restaurant. Yet each of the state\u2019s six islands has something unique worth seeing. With a bit of island hopping (which can be done by air or by boat), the best of Hawai\u2019i can be seen in one adventuresome trip.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;On top of the world in O\u2019ahu&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Many direct flights to Hawai\u2019i land at Honolulu International Airport on &lt;a title=\"Oahu, HI\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/17542217#photo/89375\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;O\u2019ahu&lt;\/a&gt;, the most populated of the islands, which makes it an easy place to start any vacation. &lt;a title=\"Waikiki Beach, Hawaii\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/2329214#photo/36493\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Waikiki&lt;\/a&gt;, the southern neighborhood of Honolulu, houses most of the resorts on &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/12439652\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;O\u2019ahu&lt;\/a&gt;. Visitors can find both modern resorts, like the &lt;a title=\"Hyatt Regency Waikiki\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/17407917\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Hyatt Regency&lt;\/a&gt;, Sheraton Waikiki, and the Hilton Hawaiian Village, as well as historic hotels like the &lt;a title=\"Moana Surfrider Hotel, Waikiki, HI\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/3800495#photo/89404\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Moana Surfrider Hotel&lt;\/a&gt;, built in 1901, and the Royal Hawaiian Hotel, built in 1927.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Thanks to its long rolling breaks, Waikiki provides beginner-friendly waves for beginning surfers. Take surf lessons from Gone Surfing Hawaii, specializing in getting beginners up on the board in their first lesson.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;While in Waikiki, try one of the restaurants inspired by Hawaii Regional Cuisine, a farm-to-table food movement started by 12 Hawaiian chefs long before farm-to-table fit into the vernacular. Restaurants like &lt;a title=\"The Pineapple Room, HI\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/10462221#photo/89406\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;The Pineapple Room&lt;\/a&gt;, Chef Mavro, and Roy\u2019s Waikiki serve dishes like nori wrapped tempura ahi, katsu curry tilapia, and macadamia nut-crusted lamb chops, highlighting local Hawaiian ingredients in innovative ways.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;In central O\u2019ahu, 30 minutes from Waikiki, &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8279043\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Pearl Harbor&lt;\/a&gt; commemorates the 2,390 men who lost their lives in the World War II attack by the Japanese through a number of historic sites. The USS Arizona memorial takes visitors in a boat shuttle over the hull of the sunken battleship, and a visitor center honors the people who lost their lives through historic film and a marble wall with their names. The &lt;a title=\"USS Bowfin Submarine Museum and Park\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/4329283\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;USS Bowfin Submarine Museum and Park&lt;\/a&gt; explores the war under water through a 10,000-square-foot space, including an authentic submarine and torpedo room.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Hanging out on the Big Island&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Known as the \u201cBig Island,\u201d Hawaii Island is bigger than all the other islands combined, and it shows in the diverse climate regions and varied landscape. Take a day trip to &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/154680\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Hawaii Volcanoes National Park&lt;\/a&gt; and see Kilauea, one of the world\u2019s most active volcanoes. The eruptions have created over 490 acres of new land, making the already-big island even bigger. The Kilauea Visitor Center offers maps, ranger talks, and eruption updates Monday through Sunday from 7:45 a.m. to 5 p.m.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The volcanic landscape also creates some spectacular black sand beaches, like &lt;a title=\"Punaluu Black Sand Beach, HI\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/93797#photo/89419\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Punaluu Black Sand Beach&lt;\/a&gt;, just 30 miles south of Hawaii Volcanoes National Park. The beach is also a favorite of green sea turtles that can sometimes be seen lounging on the sand.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;On the west side of the island, Kona coffee reigns. About 600 coffee farms take advantage of the volcanic soil and high elevation to produce coffee that tastes lighter and smoother than coffee grown elsewhere. Join the free tour at &lt;a title=\"Mountain Thunder Coffee Plantation\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/1643210#photo/89434\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Mountain Thunder Coffee Plantation&lt;\/a&gt;, which takes visitors through the process from crop to cup, and offers a 6-ounce coffee tasting at the tour\u2019s conclusion.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Keeping history in Kauai&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;The furthest island west, &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/5647503\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Kaua\u2019i&lt;\/a&gt;, is Hawai\u2019i\u2019s oldest island, and a long history of traditions\u2014and changes\u2014have accompanied that title. Get to know the island\u2019s history as a sugar plantation on the Koloa Heritage Trail, and see artifacts and art capturing the culture of the people of Kaua\u2019i at the &lt;a title=\"Kaua'i Museum, Lihue, HI\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/17542219\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Kaua\u2019i Museum&lt;\/a&gt; in Lihue.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;For a bit of natural history, the jutting cliffs of the &lt;a title=\"Na Pali Coast, Kaua'i, HI\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/93147#photo/89437\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Na Pali Coast&lt;\/a&gt; show-off the island\u2019s volcanic past as they stretch 4,000 feet above the Pacific. Inaccessible by cars, the park can only be seen by foot, kayak, or helicopter, all of which can be reserved from Kaua\u2019i\u2019s north shore towns.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Mule rides in Moloka\u2019i&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Ranked by National Geographic as having some of the highest ratings for environmental stewardship, &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8296373\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Moloka\u2019i&lt;\/a&gt; maintains much of its original landscape as well as its culture. See the tallest sea cliffs in the world, at 3,600 to 3,900 feet, on a mule ride to the &lt;a title=\"Kalaupapa National Historic Park, Kaua'i, HI\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/94745#photo/89461\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Kalaupapa National Historic Park&lt;\/a&gt;, a 34-acre area inaccessible by cars.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Little Lana\u2019i&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Once an island-wide pineapple plantation, the small island of &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8239025\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Lana\u2019i&lt;\/a&gt; has only recently been opened to tourists. The island has no street lights, but &lt;a title=\"Four Seasons Resort Lana'i, HI\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/17542247#photo/89469\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;The Four Seasons Resort Lana\u2019i &lt;\/a&gt;and the Lodge at Ko\u2019ele each operate a golf course, and outfitters supply visitors with bicycle rentals and off-road vehicles to access the island\u2019s tide pools and mountain roads.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Making tracks in Maui&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;The second largest island, &lt;a title=\"Maui, HI\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/5970444#photo/11249\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Maui&lt;\/a&gt; is covered with untouched Hawaiian land on its east side, and modern resort amenities on its west side. Galloway","owner_avatar_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/1842ae6b2c6f826a5b7affe148b36b4d","id":11516,"description":"Whether you\u2019re after photo-worthy landscape views, a glimpse
