sea.","path":"/collections/summer-bucket-list-the-5-most-iconic-american-road-trips-11516","total_likes":4,"total_photos":0,"branding_details":{"ad_magic_number":"93329696","article_content":"&lt;p&gt;Just like baseball and apple pie, the great summer road trip has been woven into the fabric of American culture. With more than 8.5 million miles of driveable roads (according to the Federal Highway Administration), the United States has no shortage of routes perfect for summer road tripping. Yet among the millions of miles, a few extra-special drives should be on every traveler\u2019s must-do summer bucket list. Whether you\u2019re after photo-worthy landscape views, a glimpse into the past, or a little bit of adventure, these iconic American road trips offer the chance to see the wide and varied country from sea to shining sea.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Pacific Coast Highway&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;See mountains meet the sea along the California coast and take 550 miles of State Route 1, better known as the Pacific Coast Highway from &lt;a title=\"Mendocino County, CA\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/18335213\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Mendocino County&lt;\/a&gt;, about 150 miles north of San Francisco, all the way to Dana Point in Orange County. Though the drive can be done in either direction, take PCH from north to south to keep the ocean closer on the right side.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The most scenic and celebrated part of the drive starts in the central coast in Monterey, once California\u2019s capital and home to the 320,000-square-foot Monterey Bay Aquarium and its famous California sea otters. About 30 miles south, the drive by Big Sur shows off the impressive waves hitting the cliffs of the Santa Lucia mountains; some areas of the road hit 1,000 feet above sea level, giving drivers an even more epic vantage point.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Continuing on, about four hours from both Los Angeles and San Francisco, the sleepy town of San Simeon plays host to the grand Hearst castle, an 165-room estate built by publishing giant William Randolph Hearst in 1947. Tours of the grand rooms, gardens, and pools usually run about 45 minutes, but an evening tour ventures across more of the estate and lasts just over two hours.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Driving the full stretch of road from northern to southern California will take about 9 hours, but riding just the Central Coast takes about 90 minutes without the scenic stops.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Route 66&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;The road that was synonymous with \u201croad trips\u201d in the 1950s, Route 66 became the favorite route for vacationers heading from the Midwest to sunny Los Angeles. The road\u2019s heavy traffic meant plenty of gas stations, quirky motels, and classic restaurants (including the first-drive thru in Springfield, Missouri) popped up to serve weary drivers.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Today a few of those roadside icons still stand, like the Wagon Wheel Motel in Cuba, Missouri, where a neon sign still greets visitors, just as it has since 1936. Eat at the 66 Diner in Albuquerque, New Mexico to hear classic songs from the \u201850s play on the jukebox and sip on milkshakes from the full soda fountain. Farther west, guests can stay in 28-foot high steel tepees at the Wigwam Village Hotel in Holbrooke, Arizona.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The drive takes about 37 hours from its origin in Chicago to Los Angeles, but can be picked up in any of the states it runs through, including Missouri, Kansas, Oklahoma, Texas, New Mexico and Arizona. Expect to spend four to five days with stops along the way.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Harriet Tubman Underground Railway Byway&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;This may not be the most recognized road trip, but the combination of antebellum history and marshy landscape of Maryland eastern shore and countryside make this drive one of America\u2019s most interesting treks. Start in Cambridge, Maryland and make a stop at the Harriet Tubman Museum and Educational Center before heading to the Long Wharf, where slaves where once brought from overseas and sold, but also an escape point where slaves could use the Delaware River to flee north.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Follow the pastoral Church Creek Road (also called the MD-16) southwest to the Chesapeake bayside town of Madison, where historians believe Harriet Tubman was born and learned skills like navigating by the stars from dock workers and the mariners who would ship timber up and down the canals. Circle back on Smithville road to Golden Hill Road, and swap the car for a bike to see the 27,000-acre Blackwater National Wildlife Refuge and its many birds and wetland wildlife up-close.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;From here, head back north until hitting MD-16, which can be taken to the MD-331 all the way to the Delaware border where the Mason-Dixon Line, marked with a crownstone today, represented one step closer to freedom for fleeing slaves.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;This 125-mile long byway isn\u2019t a straight shot, so it takes at minimum of about six hours to complete. Give it two days to completely explore all the historical stops along the way.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;North Shore Scenic Drive&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;While road trips along the coasts usually get all the glory, the road trip along America\u2019s largest lake is just as worthy of attention. The eastern Minnesota border follows the shore of Lake Superior with MN-61, starting in Duluth and ending at the Canadian border. Get oriented to the lake\u2019s shipping history at the Lake Superior Maritime Visitor Center in Duluth, then visit Glensheen, an English-style estate built in 1905 and furnished in that era\u2019s trappings (including a classic billiard room and table).&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Keep heading north to Two Harbors, Minnesota to see a relic of Lake Superior\u2019s shipping days, Edna G. Tugboat. This mighty boat served from 1896 to 1981 and was the last surviving steam tugboat to work on the Great Lakes. The Split Rock Lighthouse, built in 1909, gives visitors a look into life in a lighthouse and the importance of the building at a time when shipwrecks were all too common.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The US part of the drive comes to an end at Grand Portage (though drivers can continue up into Canada another 100 miles to reach the northernmost point of Lake Superior). Remnants of the 18&lt;sup&gt;th&lt;\/sup&gt;-century fur trade can be seen at the Great Portage National Monument, where the Ojibwe Indians share their trading history and way of life and a warehouse showcases the birch and cedar canoes that were essential for moving fur east to west. The Grand Portage State Park makes a dramatic end to the journey as drivers can get out and see High Falls, the tallest waterfall in Minnesota, and traverse down the trail to the Pigeon River below.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The trip takes about three hours when driven straight through, but allow for a full day to include stops.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Florida Overseas Highway&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Traverse the tiny islands that separate the Gulf of Mexico and the Atlantic Ocean and hop on US Route 1 to see the Florida Keys from top to bottom. Before leaving Key Largo, the start of the journey, ride a glass-bottomed boat to visit the John Pennekamp Coral Reef State Park, home to North America\u2019s only coral reef, 55 types of coral, and 600 kinds of fish. About 25 miles into the drive, take a tanning and picnic break on Anne\u2019s Beach and enjoy the turquoise waters.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;From there, keep driving until you reach Mile Marker 0, the southernmost point in the continental United States. Ernest Hemingway\u2019s home is right nearby, and descendants of his six-toed cats still roam the property.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The road finally comes to an end in Key West, where one of the oldest lighthouses in the US still stands. Walk the 88 steps of the Key West Lighthouse to see the Atlantic Ocean and Gulf of Mexico at the same time. Diving drivers should celebrate the end of the journey with a dip in Shipwreck Trail, part of the Florida Keys National Marine Sanctuary, where nine ships have sunk and left their hollowed bones below. An undersea guide can provide the history and information on the reef life.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The total drive takes about two hours from Key Largo to Key West, or a little over three hours from Miami.&lt;\/p&gt;","article_id":"2862","header_box_background_color":"#fcfdfd","header_box_text_color":null,"hero_image_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/cc59febd44b589bf8e8f0750d33f11c3","id":4061,"on_homepage":null,"page_background_color":"#b2e1ed","show_in_ca":false,"show_in_us":true,"subheader_text_color":null,"superhero_image_url":null,"tracking_pixel_1":null,"tracking_pixel_2":null,"video_id":null},"editorial":true,"travel_guide":true,"main_photo_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/f77fa7c210f0fa2830f77ec57bb8b6a6","collage_image_urls":["http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/da7f7fa689f680334447d33e9c04f68b","http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/767599cf8e3e6df5f058caac202df8fd","http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/4e873443772cef1cf73a28e813fb6ae2"]},{"type":"collection","name":"Everydayer: Kennedy Space Center, Cape Canaveral","owner_name":"MapQuest Feature Writer Lindsey Galloway","owner_avatar_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/1842ae6b2c6f826a5b7affe148b36b4d","id":722,"description":"Blast off into space (on earth) with the space shuttle simulator at the Kennedy Space Center in Cape Canaveral, Florida. The working NASA facility gets visitors up close and personal with out-of-this-world experiences.","path":"/collections/everydayer-kennedy-space-center-cape-canaveral-722","total_likes":21,"total_photos":0,"branding_details":{"ad_magic_number":"93329696","article_content":"&lt;p&gt;From the Apollo missions, to the Moon, to the launch of the space shuttles, the &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/748653\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Kennedy Space Center&lt;\/a&gt; has been home to some of the country\u2019s most memorable moments. See where this history has taken flight by making a visit to the Kennedy Space Center about 45 miles east of &lt;a title=\"Orlando, FL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7030093#photo/85489\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Orlando, Florida&lt;\/a&gt;.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The 216-square-mile facility on &lt;a title=\"Merritt Island, FL\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7024684#photo/88105\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Merritt Island, Florida&lt;\/a&gt; remains an active launch and landing location for NASA missions. Hope on a bus tour of the entire center (they depart every 15 minutes from the center\u2019s visitor complex), and check out the NASA headquarters, former shuttle launch pads and landing areas, and the Apollo/Saturn V center that showcases spacesuits and rockets from the Apollo missions. Guests can get off at certain stops throughout the tour to see the locations up-close.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;More living exhibit than stodgy museum; the 70-acre Kennedy Space Center visitor complex offers a look into the history of NASA and the Space program through interactive experiences and real-life perspectives. A former astronaut makes an appearance during the daily Astronaut Encounter and answers questions from visitors (times vary depending on the astronaut\u2019s schedule). The Shuttle Launch Experience allows guests to feel what it might be like to take off from Earth in a motion simulator, and the five-story IMAX theatre shows 45-minute films with spectacular shots from space.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Stocked with rockets instead of roses, the Rocket Garden displays the Redstone, Atlas, and Titan rockets that have sent men into space. Detailed tours of the garden occur at 10:30 a.m. and 4 p.m. Monday through Sunday. Another more recent piece of history will have a place to call home when the retired space shuttle Atlantis arrives for permanent display starting in the spring of 2013.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The Kennedy Space Center opens Monday through Friday 9 a.m., and general admission costs $50 for adults and $40 for children 3 to 11. Hop on a chairlift to make it to the top of Mount Gushmore, then take a slide on the almost-vertical Summit Plummet and its 120ft slope. This second-tallest slide in the world displays your top speed on a digital counter once you reach the bottom, and some riders clock in at speeds up to 60 miles per hour.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Boiling River, Yellowstone National Park, WY&lt;br&gt;&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Water topping 140 degrees gushes over into the Gardner River in this spot creating a mix of hot and cold water in this wonderous geological spot within Yellowstone National Park. It takes a 1.25 mile hike to get there from a parking area located on the 45&lt;sup&gt;th&lt;\/sup&gt; parallel (halfway between the North Pole and equator), but it\u2019s one of the only spots within the park where you can get in the water without getting in trouble from park rangers.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Water World, Federal Heights, CO&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;This sprawling park has plenty of fun slides and rides with no height restrictions and more family tube rides than any other water park, making it a great stop for families. Water slide with the dinosaurs on \u201cVoyage to the Center of the Earth,\u201d a raft ride through the dark prehistoric jungle with creatures at every slippery turn, or journey back to ancient Egypt on the \u201cLost River of the Pharaohs.\u201d&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Bridal Veil Falls, GA&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;These falls look just like their name as rushing white water spreads over a wide swath of rock at the bottom of the 1000ft-deep Tallulah Gorge. Snag a free day permit to gain access to the gorge floor, then hike down the river to take a trip down natural water slide created by the smooth and wide rock that creates the falls or just chill in the calm waters that follow.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Noah\u2019s Ark, Wisconsin Dells, WI&lt;br&gt;&lt;\/strong&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;With more than 50 water slides, this enormous water park (the largest in the US) has everything from a 4-D \u201cDive-In\u201d theatre to a water slide where riders go down a completely dark tube. Thrill-seekers shouldn\u2019t miss the recently opened \u201cScorpion\u2019s Tail,\u201d a nearly vertical, 10-storey slide where riders must step into a capsule before the bottom drops out from beneath them and sends them plunging feet first at 50 feet per second.&lt;\/p&gt;","article_id":"3321","header_box_background_color":"#fcfdfd","header_box_text_color":null,"hero_image_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/2ffd832c62f30ddfd2be040c1873b8ec","id":4664,"on_homepage":null,"page_background_color":"#5975b6","show_in_ca":false,"show_in_us":true,"subheader_text_color":null,"superhero_image_url":null,"tracking_pixel_1":null,"tracking_pixel_2":null,"video_id":null},"editorial":true,"travel_guide":true,"main_photo_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/14c6dde5695eaaab84be48c1c6ad11d0","collage_image_urls":["http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/db76257c8071405da544e6326be6ae61","http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/39fc09331874487e8e32703e024580e7","http://static.flickr.com/7145/6415007785_3fbd12bd2a_b.jpg"]},{"type":"collection","name":"The Long Haul: Depart to the Desert of Arizona ","owner_name":"MapQuest Feature Writer Lindsey Galloway","owner_avatar_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/1842ae6b2c6f826a5b7affe148b36b4d","id":754,"description":"Arizona\u2019s landscape may be mostly desert, but the southwestern state is anything but dry when it comes to warm-weather fun. Yet as tough and rugged as the landscape might look on the outside, destinations throughout the state have been tamed with creature comforts complete with golf courses, spas, and shopping. See both sides of the state with a long-haul trip to Arizona running north from the Grand Canyon and traveling south to Tucson and Tombstone.&lt;br&gt;\u00a0&lt;br&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Getting down in the Grand Canyon&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Arizona\u2019s nickname is \u201c&lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/1577319\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;The Grand Canyon&lt;\/a&gt;\u201d state, and for good reason. The natural wonder stretches across 277 miles and reaches over 6,000 feet deep in spots, created by the Colorado River carving its way through.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Most visitors enter the canyon at the South Rim, where the park headquarters are located along with a number of hotels and restaurants. Experienced campers can start at the less crowded North Rim from mid-May to mid-October where campsites can be booked online up to six months in advance. The entrance fee for both entry points costs $25 for vehicles and $12 for visitors traveling by foot, bicycle, or motorcycle.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Park rangers offer programs on the natural and cultural history of the Grand Canyon throughout the day, or visitors can use their cell phone for a free audio tour along different points of interest on the South Rim.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;To see the Grand Canyon from another perspective, book a raft trip through Arizona Raft Adventures or one of the many other outfitters that operate in the area. Or, book a mule tour through Xanterra Parks and Resorts. The three-hour trip and the overnight ride both book up quickly, so reservations are accepted up to a year in advance.&lt;br&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Cultural capital in Phoenix and Scottsdale&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;With low temperatures in December only getting down to 45 degrees, &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7526194\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Phoenix&lt;\/a&gt; attracts its fair share of residents and visitors alike looking to escape winter weather. On a cooler day, visit the &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/12253684\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Desert Botanical Garden&lt;\/a&gt;, the only botanical garden in the world to focus entirely on desert plants. The 145-acre garden showcases more than 21,000 plants like cactus, agave, and aloe. The garden is open Monday through Friday 9 a.m. to 8 p.m. October through April, and 7 a.m. to 8 p.m. May through September. Admission for adults costs $18, and $15 for children 12 and under.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;On a hot day (Phoenix has plenty, even in early spring), head to one of the city\u2019s museums. &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/5595912\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;The Heard Museum&lt;\/a&gt; on Central Avenue in downtown Phoenix celebrates the history and culture of American indigenous people, and in particular, the tribes of the Southwest. The galleries are open 9:30 a.m. to 5 p.m. Monday through Saturday, and 11 a.m. to 5 p.m. on Sunday, and admission costs $18 for adults and $7.50 for children 12 and under. Admission for American Indians remains free.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Deals on Hotels in Phoenix.&lt;br&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Phoenix%2C+AZ&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/the-long-haul-depart-to-the-desert-of-arizona-754&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/the-long-haul-depart-to-the-desert-of-arizona-754\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignnone\" src=\"http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"97\" height=\"31\"&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;As a suburban neighbor to the east, &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/7053677\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Scottsdale&lt;\/a&gt; specializes in the golf and resort scene. Play 18 holes at the top-ranked &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/13903461\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Troon Golf Course&lt;\/a&gt;, where courses run through natural ravines and giant boulders border the greens. Tee time rates start at $95 for four players.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Kick back after a long day in the sun at one of Scottsdale\u2019s many spas. Book the Havasupai Body Oasis Experience at the 40,000-square foot &lt;a title=\"Willow Stream Spa, Scottsdale, AZ\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/17542204\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Willow Stream spa&lt;\/a&gt;, where warm waterfalls envelop the body mimicking the Havasu falls in the Grand Canyon.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Scottsdale also has no shortage of shopping. Stop by &lt;a title=\"Old Town Scottsdale, AZ\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/4282895#photo/89284\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Old Scottsdale&lt;\/a&gt; for classic Southwest jewelry and art, or &lt;a title=\"Scottsdale Fashion Square, Scottsdale, AZ\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/6844776\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Scottsdale Fashion Square&lt;\/a&gt; for top-end brands like Barney\u2019s New York and Jimmy Choo.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Deals on Hotels in Scottsdale.&lt;br&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Scottsdale%2C+AZ&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/the-long-haul-depart-to-the-desert-of-arizona-754&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/the-long-haul-depart-to-the-desert-of-arizona-754\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignnone\" title=\"Book Now\" src=\"http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"97\" height=\"31\"&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;\u00a0&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Walking back in time in Tombstone&lt;\/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Picture the Arizona old west in its heyday by paying a visit to the tiny town of &lt;a href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/8041672\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;Tombstone&lt;\/a&gt;. Seventy miles southeast of Tucson and 30 miles north of the Mexico border, Tombstone took off when a prospector found silver. The town soon attracted prospectors, prostitutes, and others seeking a fortune, all of whom caused their fair share of trouble in town.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The town\u2019s most famous event, the Gunfight at the &lt;a title=\"OK Corral, Tombstone, AZ\" href=\"http://discover.mapquest.com/places/4283598#photo/89298\" target=\"_blank\"&gt;OK Corral&lt;\/a&gt; between Wyatt Earp, Doc Holliday and the McLaurys and Clantons, is recreated at 2 p.m. Monday through Sunday. The OK Corral stays open 9:30 a.m. to 5 p.m. with historical shows and an exhibit on The Tombstone Epitaph, the newspaper that documented the stranger-than-fiction happenings in this Arizona town.&lt;\/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Find Great Deals on Hotels in Tombstone.&lt;br&gt;&lt;a href=\"http://bookings.mapquest.com/city/?refid=5101&amp;rs_city=Tombstone%2C+AZ&amp;refclickid=inad-dscvr&amp;icid=mqinad-discover-http://discover.mapquest.com/collections/the-long-haul-depart-to-the-desert-of-arizona-754&amp;utm_source=Discover&amp;utm_medium=inad&amp;utm_campaign=http%3A//discover.mapquest.com/collections/the-long-haul-depart-to-the-desert-of-arizona-754\"&gt;&lt;img class=\"alignnone\" title=\"Book Now\" src=\"http://o.aolcdn.com/os/mapquest/marketing/email_marketing/ota/general/booknow.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"97\" height=\"31\"&gt;&lt;\/a&gt;&lt;\/p&gt;","article_id":"265","header_box_background_color":"#fcfdfd","header_box_text_color":"","hero_image_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/719a09aba22eab0c125b37459dcda51c","id":160,"on_homepage":null,"page_background_color":"#b2e1ed","show_in_ca":false,"show_in_us":true,"subheader_text_color":"","superhero_image_url":null,"tracking_pixel_1":null,"tracking_pixel_2":null,"video_id":null},"editorial":true,"travel_guide":true,"main_photo_url":"http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/a296cff3f6a3923936cffc17ae8d2f92","collage_image_urls":["http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/cedeb35127c729cd8dfb5b93d8e4347b","http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/898ecd8f166ea3cab53ab49880cfdfca","http://o.aolcdn.com/hss/storage/mqdiscover/ef437ec2176011c3e08d6234accdc47d"]}]});
